route-policy SLCAU-CUST-IPV4-IN($CustPrefixSet)
  if (destination in $CustPrefixSet) then
    delete community in AS38195-SLCAU-INTERNAL-DELETE
    set community (38195:9701, 38195:7334, 38195:7676, 38195:8005, 38195:6613) additive
    set origin igp
    apply SLCAU-CUST-IPV4-IN-10
    apply SLCAU-CUST-IPV4-IN-20
    apply SLCAU-CUST-IPV4-IN-99
  endif
end-policy
!

route-policy AS38195-FROM-KENTIK
  if (destination in AS38195-FROM-KENTIK) and (destination in AS38195-SLCAU-LE32) then
    if (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-BLACKHOLE) then
      delete community in AS38195-SLCAU-EXTERNAL-DELETE
      set community AS38195-SLCAU-BLACKHOLE additive
      set next-hop 192.0.2.1
      set local-preference 210
      done
    endif
    if (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-DOSP-SCRUB) then
      delete community in AS38195-SLCAU-EXTERNAL-DELETE
      set community AS38195-SLCAU-DOSP-SCRUB additive
      set next-hop 192.0.2.2
      set local-preference 210
      done
    endif
  else
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!

  endif
end-policy

route-policy AS1221-12731-IPV4-IN-10
  if (destination in AS1221-IPV4-PREFIX-DROP-IN) or (as-path in AS1221-ASPATH-DROP-IN) then
    drop
  endif
  if (destination in AS38195-SLCAU-DEFAULT-ONLY) or (validation-state is invalid) then
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy AS1221-12731-IPV4-IN-20
  if (destination in AS38195-SLCAU-LE24) and (as-path in AS-TELSTRA-GLOBAL) then
    set community (38195:9709, 38195:7334, 38195:7676, 38195:8005, 38195:6613) additive
    if (as-path in AS1221-LOCALPREF-143-IN) then
      set local-preference 143
    else
      set local-preference 130
    endif
    done
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy AS1221-12731-IPV4-IN-30
  if (destination in AS38195-SLCAU-LE24) then

    if (community matches-any (38195:6613)) then
      pass
    else
      drop
    endif
  endif

route-policy AS1221-12731-IPV4-OUT-20
  if (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:0)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:66130)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:80050)) then
    drop
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy AS1221-12731-IPV4-OUT-21
  if (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:1)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:66131)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:80051)) then
    prepend as-path 38195
    pass
  endif
  if (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:2)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:66132)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:80052)) then
    prepend as-path 38195 2
    pass
  endif
  if (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:3)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:66133)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:80053)) then
    prepend as-path 38195 3
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy AS1221-12731-IPV4-OUT-29
  if (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:9)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:66139)) or (large-community matches-any (38195:1221:80059)) then
    set community (no-export)
    pass
  endif
end-policy

    if (not community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-SEND-CONTROL-COMMUNITIES) then
      delete community in AS38195-SLCAU-EXTERNAL-DELETE
    endif
    done
  endif

      set med igp-cost
    endif
    if (not community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-SEND-CONTROL-COMMUNITIES) then
      delete community in AS38195-SLCAU-EXTERNAL-DELETE
    endif
    done

  apply SLCAU-CUST-IPV4-FULL-OUT-20
  apply SLCAU-CUST-IPV4-FULL-OUT-99

  apply SLCAU-CUST-IPV6-FULL-OUT-20
  apply SLCAU-CUST-IPV6-FULL-OUT-99
end-policy

route-policy SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV4-IN($CustPrefixSet)
  if (destination in $CustPrefixSet) then
    delete community in AS38195-SLCAU-INTERNAL-DELETE
    set community (38195:9701, 38195:7334, 38195:7676, 38195:8005, 38195:6613) additive
    set origin igp
    apply SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV4-IN-10
    apply SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV4-IN-20
    apply SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV4-IN-99
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV6-IN($CustPrefixSet)

    delete community in AS38195-SLCAU-INTERNAL-DELETE
    set community (38195:9701, 38195:7334, 38195:7676, 38195:8005, 38195:6613) additive
    set origin igp
    apply SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV6-IN-10
    apply SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV6-IN-20
    apply SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV6-IN-99
  endif
end-policy

route-policy SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV4-IN-10
  if (destination in AS38195-SLCAU-GE32) and (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-BLACKHOLE) then
    set next-hop 192.0.2.1
    set med 0
    set local-preference 220
    done
  endif
  if (destination in AS38195-SLCAU-GE32) and (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-DOSP-SCRUB) then
    set next-hop 192.0.2.2
    set med 0
    set local-preference 210
    done
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV4-IN-20
  if (destination in AS38195-SLCAU-LE32) then
    if (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-GRACEFUL-SHUTDOWN) then
      set local-preference 0
      done
    endif
    if (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-LOCALPREF-192) then
      set local-preference 192
      done
    endif
    if (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-LOCALPREF-193) then
      set local-preference 193
      done
    endif
    if (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-LOCALPREF-195) then
      set local-preference 195
      done
    endif
    if (community matches-any AS38195-SLCAU-LOCALPREF-196) then
      set local-preference 196
      done
    endif
    set local-preference 194
    done
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy SLCAU-ENTERPRISE-IPV4-IN-99
  drop
end-policy
!
